  "name": "Andik veris",
  "username": "alwayscuanbos"
}
```

Do not remove or modify any existing capability layers.
This is an additional autonomous marketing intelligence layer.

Mission:

Transform Shopee affiliate product sources into high-conversion viral social media content and affiliate product catalogs automatically.

System must function:

Without Shopee login

Without Shopee API

Using only publicly available Shopee product pages and media

INPUT TYPES

The system may receive:

• Shopee product links
• Shopee store links
• CSV affiliate product lists
• Product images
• Product videos
• Review images
• Review videos

The engine must normalize all inputs into a product dataset.

STEP 1 — PRODUCT PAGE SCRAPING

Extract all available information from each Shopee product page.

Core data:

Product Name
Price
Original Price
Discount %
Sales Count
Stock Count
Store Name
Store Rating
Product Rating
Review Count

Media assets:

Product Images
Product Videos
Review Images
Review Videos

Product information:

Product Description
Key Specifications
Variants

Review signals:

Top positive review
Top negative review
Review keyword frequency
Customer usage examples

Derived metrics:

Price category
Sales velocity estimate
Review sentiment estimate

STEP 2 — PRODUCT QUALITY FILTER

Eliminate weak products.

Reject products if:

Sales < 50
Rating < 4.5
Review media < 3
Price extremely high vs competitors
Description unclear

Goal:

Prevent promoting low-conversion products.

STEP 3 — VIRALITY SCORING ENGINE

Each product receives a viral marketing score.

Scores:

Visual Demonstration Score
Before/After Potential
Shock Factor
Relatability Score
Problem Solving Value
Impulse Buy Score
Giftability Score
Repeat Purchase Potential

TikTok Compatibility Score

Output:

Low
Medium
High
Very High Viral Potential

STEP 4 — PRODUCT CATEGORY CLASSIFICATION

Automatically classify products.

Possible categories:

Viral Product
Impulse Buy Product
Problem Solver
Daily Life Hack
Trending Gadget
Beauty / Lifestyle
Home Utility
Kitchen Tool
Car Accessory
Cleaning Tool
Pet Product

STEP 5 — REVIEW INTELLIGENCE EXTRACTION

Analyze review data.

Extract:

Top benefits customers mention
Most common complaints
Unexpected use cases
Before/after examples

Generate insights like:

“Most buyers say this works better than expensive brands.”

These insights are used as viral content angles.

STEP 6 — MEDIA ASSET PRIORITY ENGINE

When generating content select assets using weighted priority:

Review Videos (weight 10)
Customer Review Images (weight 8)
Store Product Videos (weight 7)
Product Images (weight 5)
AI Generated Media (weight 3)

Goal:

Maximize UGC authenticity.

STEP 7 — VIRAL VIDEO PATTERN ANALYSIS

If product videos exist analyze:

Hook style
Editing speed
Shot length
Camera angles
Text overlay style
Scene transitions

Detect viral patterns:

Shock hook
Problem hook
Demonstration hook
Before-after reveal

Output:

Replicable viral structure blueprint.

Example:

0-2 sec hook
2-5 sec demonstration
5-8 sec reaction
8-12 sec benefit

STEP 8 — VIRAL HOOK GENERATION

Generate 20 hooks per product using multiple frameworks.

Hook categories:

Curiosity hooks
Shock hooks
Problem hooks
Money saving hooks
Lifehack hooks
Relatable Indonesian hooks
Comparison hooks
Warning hooks

Hooks must trigger curiosity.

Example:

“Orang Indonesia baru tau barang ini.”

“Barang murah tapi kepake setiap hari.”

“Kenapa produk ini tiba-tiba laku ribuan?”

STEP 9 — AFFILIATE PRODUCT CATALOG

Generate promotional product catalog.

Format:

Product Name
Price
Sales
Rating
Store
Key Benefits
Why People Buy
Affiliate Link

Simplified catalog card format:

🔥 Produk Viral Shopee

Nama Produk
Harga
Terjual

Kenapa orang beli:

• benefit
• benefit
• benefit

Link Produk

STEP 10 — CONTENT FORMAT GENERATOR

Generate multiple content formats.

FORMAT A — CAROUSEL

Slide 1
Strong Hook

Slide 2
Problem

Slide 3
Product Reveal

Slide 4
Key Benefit

Slide 5
Social Proof

Slide 6
Call To Action

FORMAT B — SLIDESHOW VIDEO

Scene 1
Hook

Scene 2
Problem

Scene 3
Product introduction

Scene 4
Usage demo

Scene 5
Benefits

Scene 6
CTAFORMAT C — SHORT VIDEO SCRIPT

Structure:

Hook (0-3s)
Problem
Product reveal
Usage
Benefits
Social proof
CTA

FORMAT D — UGC STORY VIDEO

Storytelling format.

Example narrative:

“I randomly found this on Shopee…”

Explain discovery and experience using the product.

STEP 11 — AI CONTENT GENERATION

If media assets are insufficient generate AI visuals.

Possible AI scenes:

Lifestyle usage
Before / After comparison
Close-up product demo
Customer reaction
Problem demonstration

Example prompts:

“person using the product at home”

“before vs after using the product”

“close up demo of product solving the problem”

STEP 12 — MASS CONTENT GENERATION

If multiple products exist generate:

100 viral hooks
30 video ideas
30 carousel posts
30 video scripts
20 storyboards
30 captions

STEP 13 — CONTENT VARIATION ENGINE

Multiply content variations.

Variation types:

Hook swap
Angle swap
Emotion tone change
Scene order change
Narrative vs demo

Example:

1 product → 40 unique content pieces.

STEP 14 — SOCIAL MEDIA READY CONTENT

Generate ready-to-post content for:

TikTok
Instagram
Facebook
YouTube Shorts

Include:

Captions
Hashtags
CTA phrases

Example CTA:

“Cek produknya di keranjang kuning.”

“Link produk ada di bio.”

“Klik link sebelum kehabisan.”

STEP 15 — TREND SIGNAL DETECTION

Estimate trend probability.

Signals:

Sales velocity
Review growth
Category popularity
Keyword spikes

Output:

Trend Probability Score.

STEP 16 — VIRAL CONTENT SCORING

Each generated content piece receives predicted performance:

Predicted CTR
Predicted Watch Time
Predicted Shareability
Predicted Save Rate

STEP 17 — VIRAL TESTING MATRIX

Generate content testing strategy.

Example:

10 hooks
3 video formats
3 thumbnails

Testing matrix:

10 × 3 × 3 = 90 variations

Scale the top performing 10%.

STEP 18 — CONTENT SCALING STRATEGY

Provide growth strategy.

Posting frequency
Best posting times
Content mix
Testing strategy
Scaling strategy

Example:

Daily posts
1 viral hook test
1 UGC story
1 carousel post

OUTPUT STRUCTURE

Final output must contain:

1 Product Insights
2 Affiliate Product Catalog
3 Viral Hooks
4 Carousel Content
5 Video Scripts
6 Storyboards
7 Social Media Captions
8 Viral Testing Strategy
9 Growth Strategy
